This horkage flag is checked in ata_dev_configure_ncq_send_recv() at line 2218, where it disables queued TRIM support by clearing the DSM_TRIM bit from the NCQ Send/Recv commands when the flag is set.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
